	declare M.Seed : int := 1107155288 {Reuses: 0}
	declare last_rand_value : int := 0 {Reuses: 0}
	declare read randNoteValues[128] : int[] {Reuses: 0}
	i{int} := 0
	while(i{int} <= (num_elements[randNoteValues{int[]}] - 1)) 
		non_rpt_random(randNoteValues[i{int}]{int}, last_rand_value{int}, 0, 1000){UserDefined, Inlining}
		randNoteValues[i{int}]{int} := real_to_int((((int_to_real(randNoteValues[i{int}]{int}){Builtin, None} - 0) * (500 - - 500)) / (1000 - 0)) + - 500){Builtin, None}
		inc(i{int}){Builtin, None}
	end while

	mnu_preset{int} := (mnu_preset{int} + 1) mod presetCount{int}
	update.preset.menu{UserDefined, Call}
	if(presetCount{int} # 0)
		load.preset{UserDefined, Inlining}
	end if
end on

		wait_async(load_array_str(vibrato_preset{int[]}, NI_DND_ITEMS_ARRAY[0]{string}){Builtin, None}){Builtin, None}
		load.array{UserDefined, Call}
	end if
end on

on ui_control(btn_scanPresets{int})
	if(preset_scan{int} = FALSE{int})
		preset_scan{int} := TRUE{int}
		i{int} := 0
		while(i{int} <= (num_elements[vibPresetCount{int[]}] - 1)) 
			vibPresetCount[i{int}]{int} := 0
			vibPresetNames[i{int}]{string} := ""
			inc(i{int}){Builtin, None}
		end while
		array.clear(vibrato_preset2{int[]}){UserDefined, Inlining}
		array.clear(vibrato_preset{int[]}){UserDefined, Inlining}
		presetCount{int} := 0
		fs_navigate(get_ui_id(file_browser{int}){Builtin, None}, 1){Builtin, None}
	end if
end on

on ui_control(file_browser{int}){thread-unsafe}
	message("File Browser triggered"){Builtin, None}
	wait_async(load_array_str(vibrato_preset{int[]}, fs_get_filename(get_ui_id(file_browser{int}){Builtin, None}, 2){Builtin, None}){Builtin, None}){Builtin, None}
	if((preset_scan{int} = TRUE{int}) and (vibrato_preset[preset_idx.DELETED{int}]{int} # - 420))
		if(vibrato_preset[preset_idx.DELETED{int}]{int} = 0)
			if(not array_equal(vibrato_preset{int[]}, vibrato_preset2{int[]}){Builtin, None})
				vibPresetNames[presetCount{int}]{string} := fs_get_filename(get_ui_id(file_browser{int}){Builtin, None}, 0){Builtin, None}
				vibPresetCount[presetCount{int}]{int} := 1
				inc(presetCount{int}){Builtin, None}
			end if
			array.clear(vibrato_preset{int[]}){UserDefined, Inlining}
		else
			if(((vibrato_preset[preset_idx.DELETED{int}]{int} = 0) or (vibrato_preset[preset_idx.DELETED{int}]{int} = 1)) and (get_control_par(get_ui_id(btn_scanPresets{int}){Builtin, None}, CONTROL_PAR_KEY_ALT{int}){Builtin, None} = TRUE{int}))
				message("Scanning for deleted"){Builtin, None}
				if(not array_equal(vibrato_preset{int[]}, vibrato_preset2{int[]}){Builtin, None})
					vibPresetNames[presetCount{int}]{string} := fs_get_filename(get_ui_id(file_browser{int}){Builtin, None}, 0){Builtin, None}
					vibPresetCount[presetCount{int}]{int} := 1
					inc(presetCount{int}){Builtin, None}
					vibrato_preset[preset_idx.DELETED{int}]{int} := FALSE{int}
					save_array_str(vibrato_preset{int[]}, fs_get_filename(get_ui_id(file_browser{int}){Builtin, None}, 2){Builtin, None}){Builtin, None}
				end if
				array.clear(vibrato_preset{int[]}){UserDefined, Inlining}
			end if
		end if
		set_control_par(get_ui_id(btn_scanPresets{int}){Builtin, None}, CONTROL_PAR_VALUE{int}, TRUE{int}){Builtin, None}
		fs_navigate(get_ui_id(file_browser{int}){Builtin, None}, 1){Builtin, None}
	else
		message("The end"){Builtin, None}
		save.resource_arrays{UserDefined, Inlining}
		get.presetCount{UserDefined, Call}
		preset_scan{int} := FALSE{int}
		set_control_par(get_ui_id(btn_scanPresets{int}){Builtin, None}, CONTROL_PAR_VALUE{int}, FALSE{int}){Builtin, None}
		update.preset.menu{UserDefined, Call}
		load.preset{UserDefined, Inlining}
	end if
end on

on ui_control(mnu_preset{int}){thread-unsafe}
	update.preset.menu{UserDefined, Call}
	load.preset{UserDefined, Inlining}
end on

on async_complete
	if(NI_ASYNC_ID{int} = save_id{int})
		if(NI_ASYNC_EXIT_STATUS{int} = TRUE{int})
			save_id{int} := - 1
		else
			if(NI_ASYNC_EXIT_STATUS{int} = FALSE{int})
				save_id{int} := 0
			end if
		end if
	end if
	if(NI_ASYNC_ID{int} = load_id{int})
		if(NI_ASYNC_EXIT_STATUS{int} = TRUE{int})
			load_id{int} := - 1
		else
			if(NI_ASYNC_EXIT_STATUS{int} = FALSE{int})
				load_id{int} := 0
			end if
		end if
	end if
end on

function import_keyswitchArray
	i{int} := 0
	while(i{int} <= (num_elements[_keyswitch0{int[]}, Array::clip(1, 2){UserDefined, None}] - 1)) 
		j{int} := 0
		while(j{int} <= (num_elements[_keyswitch0{int[]}, Array::clip(2, 2){UserDefined, None}] - 1)) 
			if(_UI_keyswitch[(i{int} * num_elements[_keyswitch0{int[]}, 2]) + j{int}]{int} # 0)
				select(j{int})
				case keyswitch_idx.NOTE{int}
					set_control_par(_UI_keyswitch[(i{int} * num_elements[_keyswitch0{int[]}, 2]) + j{int}]{int}, CONTROL_PAR_VALUE{int}, search[keyswitches{int[]}, _keyswitch0[(i{int} * num_elements[keyswitch_idx0{int[]}]) + j{int}]{int}]){Builtin, None}
				case keyswitch_idx.NAME{int}
					set_control_par_str(_UI_keyswitch[(i{int} * num_elements[_keyswitch0{int[]}, 2]) + j{int}]{int}, CONTROL_PAR_TEXT{int}, keyswitch_names[i{int}]{string}){Builtin, None}
				case keyswitch_idx.START_GROUP{int}
					set_control_par(_UI_keyswitch[(i{int} * num_elements[_keyswitch0{int[]}, 2]) + j{int}]{int}, CONTROL_PAR_VALUE{int}, _keyswitch0[(i{int} * num_elements[keyswitch_idx0{int[]}]) + j{int}]{int} - title_groups{int}){Builtin, None}
				case keyswitch_idx.COLOR{int}
					set_control_par(_UI_keyswitch[(i{int} * num_elements[_keyswitch0{int[]}, 2]) + j{int}]{int}, CONTROL_PAR_VALUE{int}, search[key_colors{int[]}, _keyswitch0[(i{int} * num_elements[keyswitch_idx0{int[]}]) + j{int}]{int}]){Builtin, None}
				case keyswitch_idx.ACTIVATE{int} to keyswitch_idx.COLOR{int}
					set_control_par(_UI_keyswitch[(i{int} * num_elements[_keyswitch0{int[]}, 2]) + j{int}]{int}, CONTROL_PAR_VALUE{int}, _keyswitch0[(i{int} * num_elements[keyswitch_idx0{int[]}]) + j{int}]{int}){Builtin, None}
				case keyswitch_idx.PREFIX{int}
					set_control_par(_UI_keyswitch[(i{int} * num_elements[_keyswitch0{int[]}, 2]) + j{int}]{int}, CONTROL_PAR_VALUE{int}, _keyswitch0[(i{int} * num_elements[keyswitch_idx0{int[]}]) + j{int}]{int}){Builtin, None}
				case keyswitch_idx.TRANSITION{int}
					set_control_par(_UI_keyswitch[(i{int} * num_elements[_keyswitch0{int[]}, 2]) + j{int}]{int}, CONTROL_PAR_VALUE{int}, _keyswitch0[(i{int} * num_elements[keyswitch_idx0{int[]}]) + j{int}]{int}){Builtin, None}
				end select
			end if
			inc(j{int}){Builtin, None}
		end while
		inc(i{int}){Builtin, None}
	end while
end function

function update.row_fonts
	j{int} := 0
	while(j{int} <= (num_elements[_keyswitch0{int[]}, Array::clip(1, 2){UserDefined, None}] - 1)) 
		i{int} := 0
		while(i{int} <= (num_elements[_keyswitch0{int[]}, Array::clip(2, 2){UserDefined, None}] - 1)) 
			if(_UI_keyswitch[(j{int} * num_elements[_keyswitch0{int[]}, 2]) + i{int}]{int} # 0)
				set_control_par(_UI_keyswitch[(j{int} * num_elements[_keyswitch0{int[]}, 2]) + i{int}]{int}, CONTROL_PAR_FONT_TYPE{int}, _font.2pt8[get_control_par(_UI_keyswitch[j{int} * num_elements[_keyswitch0{int[]}, 2]]{int}, CONTROL_PAR_VALUE{int}){Builtin, None} * 2]{int}){Builtin, None}
			end if
			inc(i{int}){Builtin, None}
		end while
		inc(j{int}){Builtin, None}
	end while
end function

function analyze(keyswitch_idx : int){thread-unsafe}
	if(_keyswitch0[keyswitch_idx{unknown} * num_elements[keyswitch_idx0{int[]}]]{int} = TRUE{int})
		reset.keycolors{UserDefined, Call}
		get_keyrange(keyswitch_idx{unknown}){UserDefined, ParameterStack}
		fill_mapped_notes(keyswitch_idx{unknown}){UserDefined, ParameterStack}
		update.keycolor_mapped(keyswitch_idx{unknown}, _keyswitch0[(keyswitch_idx{unknown} * num_elements[keyswitch_idx0{int[]}]) + 10]{int}){UserDefined, ParameterStack}
		analyze_vibrato_groups{UserDefined, Call}
		update.keyswitch{UserDefined, Call}
	end if
end function

function analyze_vibrato_groups
	array.reset(vibrato_groups{int[]}, - 1){UserDefined, Inlining}
	ii{int} := 0
	i{int} := 0
	while(i{int} <= (12 - 1)) 
		select(_keyswitch0[(i{int} * num_elements[keyswitch_idx0{int[]}]) + 4]{int})
		case instrument.SUSTAIN{int}
			j{int} := 0
			while(j{int} <= (_keyswitch0[(i{int} * num_elements[keyswitch_idx0{int[]}]) + 5]{int} - 1)) 
				vibrato_groups[ii{int}]{int} := _keyswitch0[(i{int} * num_elements[keyswitch_idx0{int[]}]) + 3]{int} + j{int}
				inc(ii{int}){Builtin, None}
				inc(j{int}){Builtin, None}
			end while
		case instrument.LEGATO{int}
			j{int} := 0
			while(j{int} <= (((_keyswitch0[(i{int} * num_elements[keyswitch_idx0{int[]}]) + 5]{int} + title_groups{int}) + _keyswitch0[(i{int} * num_elements[keyswitch_idx0{int[]}]) + 5]{int}) - 1)) 
				vibrato_groups[ii{int}]{int} := ((_keyswitch0[(i{int} * num_elements[keyswitch_idx0{int[]}]) + 3]{int} + _keyswitch0[(i{int} * num_elements[keyswitch_idx0{int[]}]) + 6]{int}) + title_groups{int}) + j{int}
				inc(ii{int}){Builtin, None}
				inc(j{int}){Builtin, None}
			end while
		end select
		inc(i{int}){Builtin, None}
	end while
end function

function keyswitchSettings.show(Boolean : int)
	btn_keyswitchSettings{int} := Boolean{int}
	set_control_par(get_ui_id(UI_keyswitchSettings{int}){Builtin, None}, CONTROL_PAR_HIDE{int}, hide_state[Boolean{int}]{int}){Builtin, None}
end function

function fill_mapped_notes(keyswitch_idx : unknown){thread-unsafe}
	keys{int} := 0
	while(keys{int} <= 127) 
		_keyswitch_mapped_notes[(keyswitch_idx{unknown} * 128) + keys{int}]{int} := FALSE{int}
		blip_note{int} := play_note(keys{int}, 1, 0, 1){Builtin, None}
		set_event_par_arr(blip_note{int}, EVENT_PAR_ALLOW_GROUP{int}, 0, ALL_GROUPS{int}){Builtin, None}
		change_vol(blip_note{int}, - 2000000, 0){Builtin, None}
		set_event_par_arr(blip_note{int}, EVENT_PAR_ALLOW_GROUP{int}, 1, _keyswitch0[(keyswitch_idx{unknown} * num_elements[keyswitch_idx0{int[]}]) + 3]{int}){Builtin, None}
		wait(1){Builtin, None}
		zone_id{int} := get_event_par(blip_note{int}, EVENT_PAR_ZONE_ID{int}){Builtin, None}
		if(zone_id{int} # - 1)
			message(zone_id{int} & ", " & _keyswitch0[(keyswitch_idx{unknown} * num_elements[keyswitch_idx0{int[]}]) + 3]{int}){Builtin, None}
			_keyswitch_mapped_notes[(keyswitch_idx{unknown} * 128) + keys{int}]{int} := TRUE{int}
		end if
		fade_out(blip_note{int}, 0, 1){Builtin, None}
		inc(keys{int}){Builtin, None}
	end while
end function

function get_keyrange(keyswitch_idx : unknown){thread-unsafe}
	keys{int} := 0
	while(keys{int} <= 127) 
		blip_note{int} := play_note(keys{int}, 1, 0, 1){Builtin, None}
		set_event_par_arr(blip_note{int}, EVENT_PAR_ALLOW_GROUP{int}, 0, ALL_GROUPS{int}){Builtin, None}
		change_vol(blip_note{int}, - 2000000, 0){Builtin, None}
		set_event_par_arr(blip_note{int}, EVENT_PAR_ALLOW_GROUP{int}, 1, _keyswitch0[(keyswitch_idx{unknown} * num_elements[keyswitch_idx0{int[]}]) + 3]{int}){Builtin, None}
		wait(1){Builtin, None}
		zone_id{int} := get_event_par(blip_note{int}, EVENT_PAR_ZONE_ID{int}){Builtin, None}
		if(zone_id{int} # - 1)
			_keyswitch0[(keyswitch_idx{unknown} * num_elements[keyswitch_idx0{int[]}]) + 13]{int} := keys{int}
			message("Low: " & midi.note_names[keys{int}]{string}){Builtin, None}
			keys{int} := 127
		end if
		fade_out(blip_note{int}, 0, 1){Builtin, None}
		inc(keys{int}){Builtin, None}
	end while
	keys{int} := 0
	while(keys{int} <= 127) 
		blip_note{int} := play_note(127 - keys{int}, 1, 0, 1){Builtin, None}
		set_event_par_arr(blip_note{int}, EVENT_PAR_ALLOW_GROUP{int}, 0, ALL_GROUPS{int}){Builtin, None}
		change_vol(blip_note{int}, - 2000000, 0){Builtin, None}
		set_event_par_arr(blip_note{int}, EVENT_PAR_ALLOW_GROUP{int}, 1, _keyswitch0[(keyswitch_idx{unknown} * num_elements[keyswitch_idx0{int[]}]) + 3]{int}){Builtin, None}
		wait(1){Builtin, None}
		zone_id{int} := get_event_par(blip_note{int}, EVENT_PAR_ZONE_ID{int}){Builtin, None}
		if(zone_id{int} # - 1)
			_keyswitch0[(keyswitch_idx{unknown} * num_elements[keyswitch_idx0{int[]}]) + 14]{int} := 127 - keys{int}
			message("High: " & midi.note_names[127 - keys{int}]{string}){Builtin, None}
			keys{int} := 127
		end if
		fade_out(blip_note{int}, 0, 1){Builtin, None}
		inc(keys{int}){Builtin, None}
	end while
end function

function color_keyswitches
	key[0]{int} := 0
	while(key[0]{int} <= (num_elements[_keyswitch0{int[]}, Array::clip(1, 2){UserDefined, None}] - 1)) 
		set_key_color(keyswitches[key[0]{int}]{int}, KEY_COLOR_INACTIVE{int}){Builtin, None}
		if((_keyswitch0[key[0]{int} * num_elements[keyswitch_idx0{int[]}]]{int} = TRUE{int}) and (_keyswitch0[(key[0]{int} * num_elements[keyswitch_idx0{int[]}]) + 1]{int} # 127))
			set_key_color(_keyswitch0[(key[0]{int} * num_elements[keyswitch_idx0{int[]}]) + 1]{int}, KEY_COLOR_RED{int}){Builtin, None}
		end if
		inc(key[0]{int}){Builtin, None}
	end while
end function

function update.keycolor_mapped(keyswitch_idx : int, color : int)
	key[1]{int} := _keyswitch0[(keyswitch_idx{unknown} * num_elements[keyswitch_idx0{int[]}]) + 13]{int}
	while(key[1]{int} <= _keyswitch0[(keyswitch_idx{unknown} * num_elements[keyswitch_idx0{int[]}]) + 14]{int}) 
		set_key_color(key[1]{int}, KEY_COLOR_INACTIVE{int}){Builtin, None}
		if(_keyswitch_mapped_notes[(keyswitch_idx{unknown} * 128) + key[1]{int}]{int} = TRUE{int})
			set_key_color(key[1]{int}, color{int}){Builtin, None}
		end if
		inc(key[1]{int}){Builtin, None}
	end while
end function

function reset.keycolors
	key[1]{int} := 0
	while(key[1]{int} <= 127) 
		set_key_color(key[1]{int}, KEY_COLOR_INACTIVE{int}){Builtin, None}
		inc(key[1]{int}){Builtin, None}
	end while
end function

function purge.keyswitch(keyswitch_idx : int, state : int){restricted}
	start_group{int} := _keyswitch0[(keyswitch_idx{unknown} * num_elements[keyswitch_idx0{int[]}]) + 3]{int}
	num_dynamic_layers{int} := _keyswitch0[(keyswitch_idx{unknown} * num_elements[keyswitch_idx0{int[]}]) + 5]{int}
	rr_count{int} := _keyswitch0[(keyswitch_idx{unknown} * num_elements[keyswitch_idx0{int[]}]) + 6]{int}
	mic_positions{int} := _keyswitch0[(keyswitch_idx{unknown} * num_elements[keyswitch_idx0{int[]}]) + 7]{int}
	num_transitions{int} := _keyswitch0[(keyswitch_idx{unknown} * num_elements[keyswitch_idx0{int[]}]) + 8]{int}

	select(_keyswitch0[(keyswitch_idx{unknown} * num_elements[keyswitch_idx0{int[]}]) + 4]{int})
	case instrument.ONE_SHOT{int} to instrument.ADHSR{int}
		key[4]{int} := start_group{int}
		while(key[4]{int} <= ((start_group{int} + (title_groups{int} + rr_count{int})) - 1)) 
			purge_group(key[4]{int}, state{int}){Builtin, None}
			inc(key[4]{int}){Builtin, None}
		end while
	case instrument.SUSTAIN{int}
		key[4]{int} := start_group{int}
		while(key[4]{int} <= ((start_group{int} + (((title_groups{int} + num_dynamic_layers{int}) + title_groups{int}) + num_dynamic_layers{int})) - 1)) 
			purge_group(key[4]{int}, state{int}){Builtin, None}
			inc(key[4]{int}){Builtin, None}
		end while
	case instrument.LEGATO{int}
		key[4]{int} := start_group{int}
		while(key[4]{int} <= ((start_group{int} + (((((((((((title_groups{int} + rr_count{int}) + title_groups{int}) + num_dynamic_layers{int}) + title_groups{int}) + num_dynamic_layers{int}) + title_groups{int}) + (num_dynamic_layers{int} * sustain_fx{int})) + title_groups{int}) + num_transitions{int}) + title_groups{int}) + num_dynamic_layers{int})) - 1))

function array.clear(array : int[])

	while(lib.i{int} <= (num_elements[array{int[]}] - 1)) 
		array[lib.i{int}]{int} := 0
		inc(lib.i{int}){Builtin, None}
	end while
end function

function array.reset(array : int[], val : int)

	while(lib.i{int} <= (num_elements[array{[]}] - 1)) 
		array[lib.i{int}]{unknown} := val{unknown}
		inc(lib.i{int}){Builtin, None}
	end while
end function

function non_rpt_random(result : int, last_random : int, min_random : int, max_random : int)
	Rand(result{int}, min_random{int} + 1, max_random{int}){UserDefined, Inlining}
	result{int} := (last_random{int} + result{int}) mod (max_random{int} + 1)
	last_random{int} := result{int}
end function

function Rand(result : int, min : int, max : int)
	___M.Seed{int} := (8088405 * ___M.Seed{int}) + 1
	result{int} := ((sh_right(___M.Seed{int}, 8){Builtin, None} .and. 16777215) mod ((max{int} - min{int}) + 1)) + min{int}
end function

function load.array
	i{int} := preset_idx.BODY{int}
	while(i{int} <= (100 - 1)) 
		if(uiControls[i{int} - preset_idx.BODY{int}]{int} # 0)
			set_control_par(uiControls[i{int} - preset_idx.BODY{int}]{int}, CONTROL_PAR_VALUE{int}, vibrato_preset[i{int}]{int}){Builtin, None}
		end if
		inc(i{int}){Builtin, None}
	end while
	i{int} := 0
	while(i{int} <= (search[vibrato_groups{int[]}, - 1] - 1)) 
		set_engine_par(ADHSR_ENGINE_PARAMS[0]{int}, sli_envRateCurve{int}, vibrato_groups[i{int}]{int}, find_mod(vibrato_groups[i{int}]{int}, "ENV_AHDSR"){Builtin, None}, - 1){Builtin, None}
		inc(i{int}){Builtin, None}
	end while
	tbl_rate.curve{int} := sli_envRateCurve{int}
	tbl_rate.attack_point{real} := pow(10, (log(1.5){Builtin, None} / log(10){Builtin, None}) + ((((int_to_real(tbl_rate.NUM_TABLE_STEPS0{int}){Builtin, None} * 0.51) - 0) / (int_to_real(tbl_rate.NUM_TABLE_STEPS0{int}){Builtin, None} - 0)) * ((log(0.056){Builtin, None} / log(10){Builtin, None}) - (log(1.5){Builtin, None} / log(10){Builtin, None})))){Builtin, None}
	tbl_rate.release_idx{int} := real_to_int(int_to_real(tbl_rate.NUM_TABLE_STEPS0{int}){Builtin, None} * 0.75){Builtin, None}
	tbl_rate.attack{real} := (((int_to_real(sli_envRateAttack{int}){Builtin, None} - 0) * (tbl_rate.attack_point{real} - 1.5)) / (1e+06 - 0)) + 1.5
	tbl_rate.hold{int} := (((sli_envRateHold{int} - 0) * (real_to_int(int_to_real(tbl_rate.NUM_TABLE_STEPS0{int}){Builtin, None} * 0.15){Builtin, None} - 0)) / (1000000 - 0)) + 0
	tbl_rate.decay{real} := (((int_to_real(sli_envRateDecay{int}){Builtin, None} - 0) * (15000 - 800)) / (1e+06 - 0)) + 800
	tbl_rate.sustain{int} := (((sli_envRateSustain{int} - 0) * (1000 - 0)) / (1000000 - 0)) + 0
	tbl_rate.release{real} := (((int_to_real(750000){Builtin, None} - 0) * (40000 - 800)) / (1e+06 - 0)) + 800
	i{int} := 0

function sustain(event_note : int, event_notes : int, event_velocity : int, note_id : int, start_group : int, num_dynamic_layers : int, num_rr : int)
	if(event_notes{int} = - 1)
		event_notes{int} := event_note{int}
		note_id{int} := play_note(event_note{int}, event_velocity{int}, 0, 0){Builtin, None}
		set_event_par_arr(note_id{int}, EVENT_PAR_ALLOW_GROUP{int}, 0, ALL_GROUPS{int}){Builtin, None}
		dyn{int} := 0
		while(dyn{int} <= (num_dynamic_layers{int} - 1)) 
			set_event_par_arr(note_id{int}, EVENT_PAR_ALLOW_GROUP{int}, 1, dyn{int} + start_group{int}){Builtin, None}
			inc(dyn{int}){Builtin, None}
		end while
	end if
end function

function sustain_release(release_note : int, event_notes : int, note_id : int, release_id : int, start_group : int, num_dynamic_layers : int, num_rr : int)
	if(note_id{int} # - 1)
		note_off(note_id{int}){Builtin, None}
		release_id{int} := play_note(release_note{int}, 50, 0, 0){Builtin, None}
		set_event_par_arr(release_id{int}, EVENT_PAR_ALLOW_GROUP{int}, 0, ALL_GROUPS{int}){Builtin, None}
		dyn_release{int} := 0
		while(dyn_release{int} <= (num_dynamic_layers{int} - 1)) 
			set_event_par_arr(release_id{int}, EVENT_PAR_ALLOW_GROUP{int}, 1, ((dyn_release{int} + start_group{int}) + num_dynamic_layers{int}) + title_groups{int}){Builtin, None}
			inc(dyn_release{int}){Builtin, None}
		end while
		note_id{int} := - 1
		event_notes{int} := - 1
	end if
end function

function one_shot(event_note : int, event_notes : int, event_velocity : int, note_id : int, start_group : int, num_rr : int, rr_counter : int, sample_duration : int)
	if(event_notes{unknown} # event_note{int})
		event_notes{int} := event_note{int}
		rr_counter{int} := (rr_counter{int} + 1) mod num_rr{int}
		note_id{int} := play_note(event_note{int}, event_velocity{int}, 0, sample_duration{int}){Builtin, None}
		set_event_par_arr(note_id{int}, EVENT_PAR_ALLOW_GROUP{int}, 0, ALL_GROUPS{int}){Builtin, None}
		set_event_par_arr(note_id{int}, EVENT_PAR_ALLOW_GROUP{int}, 1, rr_counter{int} + start_group{int}){Builtin, None}
	end if
end function

function one_shot_release(release_note : int, event_notes : int, note_id : int)
	note_id{int} := - 1
	event_notes{int} := - 1
end function

function legato.init_arrays
	i{int} := 0
	while(i{int} <= (2000 - 1)) 
		if(sus_release_time[i{int}]{int} = 0)
			sus_release_time[i{int}]{int} := DEFAULT_VAL.sus_release_time{int}
		end if
		if(trans_fadeIn_time[i{int}]{int} = 0)
			trans_fadeIn_time[i{int}]{int} := DEFAULT_VAL.trans_fadeIn_time{int}
		end if
		if(trans_fadeOut_time[i{int}]{int} = 0)
			trans_fadeOut_time[i{int}]{int} := DEFAULT_VAL.trans_fadeOut_time{int}
		end if
		if(trans_wait_time[i{int}]{int} = 0)
			trans_wait_time[i{int}]{int} := DEFAULT_VAL.trans_wait_time{int}
		end if
		if(sus_fadeIn_time[i{int}]{int} = 0)
			sus_fadeIn_time[i{int}]{int} := DEFAULT_VAL.sus_fadeIn_time{int}
		end if
		if(trans_zone_ids[i{int}]{int} = 0)
			trans_zone_ids[i{int}]{int} := - 1
		end if
		inc(i{int}){Builtin, None}
	end while
end function

function get_trans_idx(result : int, event_id : int)
	if(search[trans_zone_ids{int[]}, (sh_left(lsb(abs(trans_group{int} - get_zone_par(get_event_par(event_id{int}, EVENT_PAR_ZONE_ID{int}){Builtin, None}, ZONE_PAR_GROUP{int}){Builtin, None}){Builtin, None}){Builtin, None}, 14){Builtin, None} .or. sh_left(lsb(get_zone_par(get_event_par(event_id{int}, EVENT_PAR_ZONE_ID{int}){Builtin, None}, ZONE_PAR_HIGH_VELO{int}){Builtin, None}){Builtin, None}, 7){Builtin, None}) .or. lsb(get_zone_par(get_event_par(event_id{int}, EVENT_PAR_ZONE_ID{int}){Builtin, None}, ZONE_PAR_ROOT_KEY{int}){Builtin, None}){Builtin, None}] = - 1)
		result{int} := search[trans_zone_ids{int[]}, - 1]
	else
		result{int} := search[trans_zone_ids{int[]}, (sh_left(lsb(abs(trans_group{int} - get_zone_par(get_event_par(event_id{int}, EVENT_PAR_ZONE_ID{int}){Builtin, None}, ZONE_PAR_GROUP{int}){Builtin, None}){Builtin, None}){Builtin, None}, 14){Builtin, None} .or. sh_left(lsb(get_zone_par(get_event_par(event_id{int}, EVENT_PAR_ZONE_ID{int}){Builtin, None}, ZONE_PAR_HIGH_VELO{int}){Builtin, None}){Builtin, None}, 7){Builtin, None}) .or. lsb(get_zone_par(get_event_par(event_id{int}, EVENT_PAR_ZONE_ID{int}){Builtin, None}, ZONE_PAR_ROOT_KEY{int}){Builtin, None}){Builtin, None}]
	end if
end function

function legato(note : int, event_notes : int, note_id : int, old_note_id : int, start_group : int, num_dynamic_layers : int, num_rr : int, trans_groups : int, sustain_fx : int, current_trans_group : int, rr_counter : int){thread-unsafe}
	atk_group{int} := start_group{number}
	atk_sus_group{int} := (atk_group{int} + num_rr{int}) + title_groups{int}
	sus_group{int} := (atk_sus_group{int} + num_dynamic_layers{int}) + title_groups{int}
	sus_fx_group{int} := (sus_group{int} + num_dynamic_layers{int}) + title_groups{int}
	trans_group{int} := (sus_fx_group{int} + (num_dynamic_layers{int} * sustain_fx{int})) + title_groups{int}
	sus_rls_group{int} := (trans_group{int} + trans_groups{int}) + title_groups{int}
	num_notes{int} := 0
	message(keyswitches[12 - 1]{int} + 1){Builtin, None}
	i{int} := keyswitches[12 - 1]{int} + 1
	while(i{int} <= (num_elements[KEY_DOWN{int[]}] - 1)) 
		num_notes{int} := KEY_DOWN[i{int}]{int} + num_notes{int}
		inc(i{int}){Builtin, None}
	end while
	message("num_notes: " & num_notes{int}){Builtin, None}
	interval{int} := EVENT_NOTE{int} - last_note{int}
	if(((num_notes{int} > 1) and (note{int} # last_note{int})) and (is_attack{int} # - 1))
		is_attack{int} := FALSE{int}
		if(abs(interval{int}){Builtin, None} <= 12)
			blip_note{int} := play_note((note{int} * abs(sh_right(abs(sh_right(interval{int} - 0, 31){Builtin, None} + 1){Builtin, None} - 1, 31){Builtin, None}){Builtin, None}) + (last_note{int} * (sh_right(interval{int} - 0, 31){Builtin, None} + 1)), (abs(interval{int}){Builtin, None} * 5) + ((sh_right(interval{int} - 0, 31){Builtin, None} + 1) * 60), 0, - 1){Builtin, None}
			change_vol(blip_note{int}, - 200000, 0){Builtin, None}
			set_event_par_arr(blip_note{int}, EVENT_PAR_ALLOW_GROUP{int}, 0, ALL_GROUPS{int}){Builtin, None}
			set_event_par_arr(blip_note{int}, EVENT_PAR_ALLOW_GROUP{int}, 1, trans_group{int} + current_trans_group{int}){Builtin, None}
			wait(1){Builtin, None}
			get_trans_idx(trans_idx{int}, blip_note{int}){UserDefined, ParameterStack}
			fade_out(old_note_id{int}, sus_release_time[trans_idx{int}]{int} * 1000, 1){Builtin, None}
			old_note_id{int} := - 1
			fade_out(last_transition{int}, 240000, 1){Builtin, None}
			fade_out(blip_note{int}, 1, 1){Builtin, None}
			transition_id{int} := play_note((note{int} * abs(sh_right(abs(sh_right(interval{int} - 0, 31){Builtin, None} + 1){Builtin, None} - 1, 31){Builtin, None}){Builtin, None}) + (last_note{int} * (sh_right(interval{int} - 0, 31){Builtin, None} + 1)), (abs(interval{int}){Builtin, None} * 5) + ((sh_right(interval{int} - 0, 31){Builtin, None} + 1) * 60), real_to_int((int_to_real(trans_zone_start[trans_idx{int}]{int}){Builtin, None} / 48000) * 1e+06){Builtin, None}, 0){Builtin, None}
			set_event_par_arr(transition_id{int}, EVENT_PAR_ALLOW_GROUP{int}, 0, ALL_GROUPS{int}){Builtin, None}
			set_event_par_arr(transition_id{int}, EVENT_PAR_MOD_VALUE_ID{int}, trans_fadeIn_time[trans_idx{int}]{int}, 3){Builtin, None}
			set_event_par_arr(transition_id{int}, EVENT_PAR_MOD_VALUE_ID{int}, trans_fadeOut_time[trans_idx{int}]{int}, 5){Builtin, None}
			set_event_par_arr(transition_id{int}, EVENT_PAR_ALLOW_GROUP{int}, 1, trans_group{int} + current_trans_group{int}){Builtin, None}
			change_vol(transition_id{int}, trans_event_volume[trans_idx{int}]{int}, 0){Builtin, None}
			note_id{int} := play_note(note{int}, 69, sus_s_start{int}, - 1){Builtin, None}
			set_event_par_arr(note_id{int}, EVENT_PAR_MOD_VALUE_ID{int}, trans_wait_time[trans_idx{int}]{int}, 0){Builtin, None}
			set_event_par_arr(note_id{int}, EVENT_PAR_MOD_VALUE_ID{int}, sus_fadeIn_time[trans_idx{int}]{int}, 2){Builtin, None}
			set_event_par_arr(note_id{int}, EVENT_PAR_ALLOW_GROUP{int}, 0, ALL_GROUPS{int}){Builtin, None}
			i{int} := 0
			while(i{int} <= (num_dynamic_layers{int} - 1)) 
				set_event_par_arr(note_id{int}, EVENT_PAR_ALLOW_GROUP{int}, 1, i{int} + sus_group{int}){Builtin, None}
				inc(i{int}){Builtin, None}
			end while
			i{int} := 0
			while(i{int} <= ((num_dynamic_layers{int} * sustain_fx{int}) - 1)) 
				set_event_par_arr(note_id{int}, EVENT_PAR_ALLOW_GROUP{int}, 1, i{int} + sus_fx_group{int}){Builtin, None}
				inc(i{int}){Builtin, None}
			end while
		else
			fade_out(old_note_id{int}, 152 * 1000, 1){Builtin, None}
			old_note_id{int} := - 1
			note_id{int} := play_note(note{int}, EVENT_VELOCITY{int}, sus_s_start{int}, - 1){Builtin, None}
			set_event_par_arr(note_id{int}, EVENT_PAR_MOD_VALUE_ID{int}, 150000, 0){Builtin, None}
			set_event_par_arr(note_id{int}, EVENT_PAR_MOD_VALUE_ID{int}, DEFAULT_VAL.sus_fadeIn_time{int}, 2){Builtin, None}
			set_event_par_arr(note_id{int}, EVENT_PAR_ALLOW_GROUP{int}, 0, ALL_GROUPS{int}){Builtin, None}
			i{int} := 0
			while(i{int} <= (num_dynamic_layers{int} - 1)) 
				set_event_par_arr(note_id{int}, EVENT_PAR_ALLOW_GROUP{int}, 1, i{int} + sus_group{int}){Builtin, None}
				inc(i{int}){Builtin, None}
			end while
			i{int} := 0
			while(i{int} <= ((num_dynamic_layers{int} * sustain_fx{int}) - 1)) 
				set_event_par_arr(note_id{int}, EVENT_PAR_ALLOW_GROUP{int}, 1, i{int} + sus_fx_group{int}){Builtin, None}
				inc(i{int}){Builtin, None}
			end while
		end if
	else
		if(num_notes{int} = 1)
			message("Initial Note"){Builtin, None}
			last_note{int} := note{int}
			is_attack{int} := - 1
			set_event_par_arr(ALL_EVENTS{int}, EVENT_PAR_ALLOW_GROUP{int}, 0, ALL_GROUPS{int}){Builtin, None}
			is_attack{int} := abs(sh_right(abs(NOTE_HELD{int}){Builtin, None} - 1, 31){Builtin, None}){Builtin, None}
			note_id{int} := play_note(note{int}, 69, 250000, - 1){Builtin, None}
			attack_id{int} := play_note(note{int}, (((EVENT_VELOCITY{int} * (1 + (sh_right((CC[103]{int} + 20) - EVENT_VELOCITY{int}, 31){Builtin, None} .or. sh_right(EVENT_VELOCITY{int} - (CC[103]{int} - 20), 31){Builtin, None}))) - ((CC[103]{int} - 20) * sh_right(EVENT_VELOCITY{int} - (CC[103]{int} - 20), 31){Builtin, None})) - ((CC[103]{int} + 20) * sh_right((CC[103]{int} + 20) - EVENT_VELOCITY{int}, 31){Builtin, None})) - (((((EVENT_VELOCITY{int} * (1 + (sh_right((CC[103]{int} + 20) - EVENT_VELOCITY{int}, 31){Builtin, None} .or. sh_right(EVENT_VELOCITY{int} - (CC[103]{int} - 20), 31){Builtin, None}))) - ((CC[103]{int} - 20) * sh_right(EVENT_VELOCITY{int} - (CC[103]{int} - 20), 31){Builtin, None})) - ((CC[103]{int} + 20) * sh_right((CC[103]{int} + 20) - EVENT_VELOCITY{int}, 31){Builtin, None})) - 127) .and. sh_right(127 - (((EVENT_VELOCITY{int} * (1 + (sh_right((CC[103]{int} + 20) - EVENT_VELOCITY{int}, 31){Builtin, None} .or. sh_right(EVENT_VELOCITY{int} - (CC[103]{int} - 20), 31){Builtin, None}))) - ((CC[103]{int} - 20) * sh_right(EVENT_VELOCITY{int} - (CC[103]{int} - 20), 31){Builtin, None})) - ((CC[103]{int} + 20) * sh_right((CC[103]{int} + 20) - EVENT_VELOCITY{int}, 31){Builtin, None})), 31){Builtin, None}), 0, 0){Builtin, None}
			set_event_par_arr(note_id{int}, EVENT_PAR_ALLOW_GROUP{int}, 0, ALL_GROUPS{int}){Builtin, None}
			key[5]{int} := 0
			while(key[5]{int} <= (num_dynamic_layers{int} - 1)) 
				set_event_par_arr(note_id{int}, EVENT_PAR_ALLOW_GROUP{int}, 1, key[5]{int} + atk_sus_group{int}){Builtin, None}
				inc(key[5]{int}){Builtin, None}
			end while
			key[5]{int} := 0
			while(key[5]{int} <= ((num_dynamic_layers{int} * sustain_fx{int}) - 1)) 
				set_event_par_arr(note_id{int}, EVENT_PAR_ALLOW_GROUP{int}, 1, key[5]{int} + sus_fx_group{int}){Builtin, None}
				inc(key[5]{int}){Builtin, None}
			end while
			set_event_par_arr(attack_id{int}, EVENT_PAR_ALLOW_GROUP{int}, 1, atk_group{int} + rr_counter{int}){Builtin, None}
			rr_counter{int} := (rr_counter{int} + 1) mod num_rr{int}
		else
			note_off(note_id{int}){Builtin, None}
		end if
	end if
	last_transition{int} := transition_id{int}
	last_note{int} := note{int}
	event_notes{int} := note{int}
end function

function legato_release(release_note : int, event_notes : int, note_id : int, release_id : int, start_group : int, num_dynamic_layers : int, num_rr : int, trans_groups : int)
	if((note_held{int} = 0) and (note_id{int} # - 1))
		event_notes{int} := - 1
		note_id{int} := - 1
		count{int} := 0
		if(is_attack{int} = FALSE{int})
			release_id{int} := play_note(get_event_par(note_id{int}, EVENT_PAR_NOTE{int}){Builtin, None}, 50, 0, 0){Builtin, None}
			set_event_par_arr(release_id{int}, EVENT_PAR_ALLOW_GROUP{int}, 0, ALL_GROUPS{int}){Builtin, None}
			key[6]{int} := 0
			while(key[6]{int} <= (num_dynamic_layers{int} - 1)) 
				set_event_par_arr(release_id{int}, EVENT_PAR_ALLOW_GROUP{int}, 1, ((((((((((key[6]{int} + start_group{int}) + num_rr{int}) + title_groups{int}) + num_dynamic_layers{int}) + title_groups{int}) + num_dynamic_layers{int}) + title_groups{int}) + (num_dynamic_layers{int} * sustain_fx{int})) + title_groups{int}) + trans_groups{int}) + title_groups{int}){Builtin, None}
				inc(key[6]{int}){Builtin, None}
			end while
		end if
		playpos{int} := (((get_event_par(note_id{int}, EVENT_PAR_PLAY_POS{int}){Builtin, None} / 10) * (1 + (sh_right(140000 - (get_event_par(note_id{int}, EVENT_PAR_PLAY_POS{int}){Builtin, None} / 10), 31){Builtin, None} .or. sh_right((get_event_par(note_id{int}, EVENT_PAR_PLAY_POS{int}){Builtin, None} / 10) - 0, 31){Builtin, None}))) - (0 * sh_right((get_event_par(note_id{int}, EVENT_PAR_PLAY_POS{int}){Builtin, None} / 10) - 0, 31){Builtin, None})) - (140000 * sh_right(140000 - (get_event_par(note_id{int}, EVENT_PAR_PLAY_POS{int}){Builtin, None} / 10), 31){Builtin, None})
		fade_out(note_id{int}, real_to_int((((int_to_real(playpos{int}){Builtin, None} - 0) * (230000 - 1)) / (140000 - 0)) + 1){Builtin, None}, 1){Builtin, None}
		change_vol(release_id{int}, - real_to_int((((int_to_real(playpos{int}){Builtin, None} - 0) * (500 - 10000)) / (140000 - 0)) + 10000){Builtin, None}, 0){Builtin, None}
		get_event_ids(active_ids{int[]}){Builtin, None}
		key[6]{int} := 0
		while(key[6]{int} <= (num_elements[active_ids{int[]}] - 1)) 
			if(not ((note_id{int} = active_ids[key[6]{int}]{int}) or (release_id{int} = active_ids[key[6]{int}]{int})))
				fade_out(active_ids[key[6]{int}]{int}, 250000, 1){Builtin, None}
			end if
			inc(key[6]{int}){Builtin, None}
		end while
	end if
end function

function find_key_nka(result : string, array : int[], nka : string, key : int, parent_folder : string, search_depth : int){restricted}
	declare local path : string {Reuses: 0}
	declare local it : int {Reuses: 0}
	array[0]{int} := - 1
	it{int} := 0
	path{string} := ""
	_id{int} := load_array_str(array{int[]}, get_folder(GET_FOLDER_PATCH_DIR{int}){Builtin, None} & path{string} & parent_folder{unknown} & nka{unknown} & ".nka"){Builtin, None}
	while(((_id{int} # - 1) and (it{int} < search_depth{int})) and (array[0]{int} # key{int})) 
		array[0]{int} := - 1
		path{string} := path{string} & "../"
		_id{int} := load_array_str(array{int[]}, get_folder(GET_FOLDER_PATCH_DIR{int}){Builtin, None} & path{string} & parent_folder{unknown} & nka{unknown} & ".nka"){Builtin, None}
		inc(it{int}){Builtin, None}
	end while
	result{string} := get_folder(GET_FOLDER_PATCH_DIR{int}){Builtin, None} & path{string} & nka{unknown} & ".nka"
end function

function Array::clip(x : int, b : int)
	return (x{int} + ((- x{int} .and. sh_right(x{int}, 31){Builtin, None}) + ((x{int} - b{int}) .and. sh_right(b{int} - x{int}, 31){Builtin, None})))
end function
